\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    \usepackage[breakable]{tcolorbox}
    \usepackage{parskip} % Stop auto-indenting (to mimic markdown behaviour)
    

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % Keep aspect ratio if custom image width or height is specified
    \setkeys{Gin}{keepaspectratio}
    % Maintain compatibility with old templates. Remove in nbconvert 6.0
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionFormat{nocaption}{}
    \captionsetup{format=nocaption,aboveskip=0pt,belowskip=0pt}

    \usepackage{float}
    \floatplacement{figure}{H} % forces figures to be placed at the correct location
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro

    \usepackage{iftex}
    \ifPDFTeX
        \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
        \IfFileExists{alphabeta.sty}{
              \usepackage{alphabeta}
          }{
              \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs}
              \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc}
          }
    \else
        \usepackage{fontspec}
        \usepackage{unicode-math}
    \fi

    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics
                         % to support a larger range
    \makeatletter % fix for old versions of grffile with XeLaTeX
    \@ifpackagelater{grffile}{2019/11/01}
    {
      % Do nothing on new versions
    }
    {
      \def\Gread@@xetex#1{%
        \IfFileExists{"\Gin@base".bb}%
        {\Gread@eps{\Gin@base.bb}}%
        {\Gread@@xetex@aux#1}%
      }
    }
    \makeatother
    \usepackage[Export]{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size
    \adjustboxset{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}

    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    % The default LaTeX title has an obnoxious amount of whitespace. By default,
    % titling removes some of it. It also provides customization options.
    \usepackage{titling}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage{array}     % table support for pandoc >= 2.11.3
    \usepackage{calc}      % table minipage width calculation for pandoc >= 2.11.1
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines
    \usepackage{soul}      % strikethrough (\st) support for pandoc >= 3.0.0
    \usepackage{mathrsfs}
    

    
    % Colors for the hyperref package
    \definecolor{urlcolor}{rgb}{0,.145,.698}
    \definecolor{linkcolor}{rgb}{.71,0.21,0.01}
    \definecolor{citecolor}{rgb}{.12,.54,.11}

    % ANSI colors
    \definecolor{ansi-black}{HTML}{3E424D}
    \definecolor{ansi-black-intense}{HTML}{282C36}
    \definecolor{ansi-red}{HTML}{E75C58}
    \definecolor{ansi-red-intense}{HTML}{B22B31}
    \definecolor{ansi-green}{HTML}{00A250}
    \definecolor{ansi-green-intense}{HTML}{007427}
    \definecolor{ansi-yellow}{HTML}{DDB62B}
    \definecolor{ansi-yellow-intense}{HTML}{B27D12}
    \definecolor{ansi-blue}{HTML}{208FFB}
    \definecolor{ansi-blue-intense}{HTML}{0065CA}
    \definecolor{ansi-magenta}{HTML}{D160C4}
    \definecolor{ansi-magenta-intense}{HTML}{A03196}
    \definecolor{ansi-cyan}{HTML}{60C6C8}
    \definecolor{ansi-cyan-intense}{HTML}{258F8F}
    \definecolor{ansi-white}{HTML}{C5C1B4}
    \definecolor{ansi-white-intense}{HTML}{A1A6B2}
    \definecolor{ansi-default-inverse-fg}{HTML}{FFFFFF}
    \definecolor{ansi-default-inverse-bg}{HTML}{000000}

    % common color for the border for error outputs.
    \definecolor{outerrorbackground}{HTML}{FFDFDF}

    % commands and environments needed by pandoc snippets
    % extracted from the output of `pandoc -s`
    \providecommand{\tightlist}{%
      \setlength{\itemsep}{0pt}\setlength{\parskip}{0pt}}
    \DefineVerbatimEnvironment{Highlighting}{Verbatim}{commandchars=\\\{\}}
    % Add ',fontsize=\small' for more characters per line
    \newenvironment{Shaded}{}{}
    \newcommand{\KeywordTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.00,0.44,0.13}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\DataTypeTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.56,0.13,0.00}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\DecValTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.63,0.44}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\BaseNTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.63,0.44}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\FloatTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.63,0.44}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\CharTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\StringTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\CommentTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textit{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\OtherTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.00,0.44,0.13}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\AlertTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{1.00,0.00,0.00}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\FunctionTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.02,0.16,0.49}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\RegionMarkerTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\ErrorTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{1.00,0.00,0.00}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\NormalTok}[1]{{#1}}

    % Additional commands for more recent versions of Pandoc
    \newcommand{\ConstantTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.53,0.00,0.00}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\SpecialCharTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\VerbatimStringTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\SpecialStringTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.73,0.40,0.53}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\ImportTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\DocumentationTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.73,0.13,0.13}{\textit{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\AnnotationTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \newcommand{\CommentVarTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \newcommand{\VariableTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.10,0.09,0.49}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\ControlFlowTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.00,0.44,0.13}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\OperatorTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.40,0.40,0.40}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\BuiltInTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\ExtensionTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\PreprocessorTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.74,0.48,0.00}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\AttributeTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.49,0.56,0.16}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\InformationTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \newcommand{\WarningTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \makeatletter
    \newsavebox\pandoc@box
    \newcommand*\pandocbounded[1]{%
      \sbox\pandoc@box{#1}%
      % scaling factors for width and height
      \Gscale@div\@tempa\textheight{\dimexpr\ht\pandoc@box+\dp\pandoc@box\relax}%
      \Gscale@div\@tempb\linewidth{\wd\pandoc@box}%
      % select the smaller of both
      \ifdim\@tempb\p@<\@tempa\p@
        \let\@tempa\@tempb
      \fi
      % scaling accordingly (\@tempa < 1)
      \ifdim\@tempa\p@<\p@
        \scalebox{\@tempa}{\usebox\pandoc@box}%
      % scaling not needed, use as it is
      \else
        \usebox{\pandoc@box}%
      \fi
    }
    \makeatother

    % Define a nice break command that doesn't care if a line doesn't already
    % exist.
    \def\br{\hspace*{\fill} \\* }
    % Math Jax compatibility definitions
    \def\gt{>}
    \def\lt{<}
    \let\Oldtex\TeX
    \let\Oldlatex\LaTeX
    \renewcommand{\TeX}{\textrm{\Oldtex}}
    \renewcommand{\LaTeX}{\textrm{\Oldlatex}}
    % Document parameters
    % Document title
    \title{Human\_Segmentation}
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
% Pygments definitions
\makeatletter
\def\PY@reset{\let\PY@it=\relax \let\PY@bf=\relax%
    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}
\def\PY@tok#1{\csname PY@tok@#1\endcsname}
\def\PY@toks#1+{\ifx\relax#1\empty\else%
    \PY@tok{#1}\expandafter\PY@toks\fi}
\def\PY@do#1{\PY@bc{\PY@tc{\PY@ul{%
    \PY@it{\PY@bf{\PY@ff{#1}}}}}}}
\def\PY#1#2{\PY@reset\PY@toks#1+\relax+\PY@do{#2}}

\def\PYZbs{\char`\\}
\def\PYZus{\char`\_}
\def\PYZob{\char`\{}
\def\PYZcb{\char`\}}
\def\PYZca{\char`\^}
\def\PYZam{\char`\&}
\def\PYZlt{\char`\<}
\def\PYZgt{\char`\>}
\def\PYZsh{\char`\#}
\def\PYZpc{\char`\%}
\def\PYZdl{\char`\$}

    % For linebreaks inside Verbatim environment from package fancyvrb.
    \makeatletter
        \newbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox
        \newbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox
        \newcommand*\Wrappedvisiblespace {\textcolor{red}{\textvisiblespace}}
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol {\textcolor{red}{\llap{\tiny$\m@th\hookrightarrow$}}}
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationindent {3ex }
        \newcommand*\Wrappedafterbreak {\kern\Wrappedcontinuationindent\copy\Wrappedcontinuationbox}
        % Take advantage of the already applied Pygments mark-up to insert
        % potential linebreaks for TeX processing.
        %        {, <, #, %, $, ' and ": go to next line.
        %        _, }, ^, &, >, - and ~: stay at end of broken line.
        % Use of \textquotesingle for straight quote.
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatspecials {%
            \def\PYGZus{\discretionary{\char`\_}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\_}}%
            \def\PYGZob{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\{}{\char`\{}}%
            \def\PYGZcb{\discretionary{\char`\}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\}}}%
            \def\PYGZca{\discretionary{\char`\^}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\^}}%
            \def\PYGZam{\discretionary{\char`\&}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\&}}%
            \def\PYGZlt{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\<}{\char`\<}}%
            \def\PYGZgt{\discretionary{\char`\>}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\>}}%
            \def\PYGZsh{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\#}{\char`\#}}%
            \def\PYGZpc{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\%}{\char`\%}}%
            \def\PYGZdl{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\$}{\char`\$}}%
            \def\PYGZhy{\discretionary{\char`\-}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\-}}%
            \def\PYGZsq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\textquotesingle}{\textquotesingle}}%
            \def\PYGZdq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\"}{\char`\"}}%
            \def\PYGZti{\discretionary{\char`\~}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\~}}%
        }
        % Some characters . , ; ? ! / are not pygmentized.
        % This macro makes them "active" and they will insert potential linebreaks
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatpunct {%
            \lccode`\~`\.\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\.}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\.}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\,\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\,}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\,}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\;\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\;}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\;}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\:\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\:}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\:}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\?\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\?}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\?}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\!\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\!}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\!}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\/\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\/}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\/}}}%
            \catcode`\.\active
            \catcode`\,\active
            \catcode`\;\active
            \catcode`\:\active
            \catcode`\?\active
            \catcode`\!\active
            \catcode`\/\active
            \lccode`\~`\~
        }
    \makeatother

    \let\OriginalVerbatim=\Verbatim
    \makeatletter
    \renewcommand{\Verbatim}[1][1]{%
        %\parskip\z@skip
        \sbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox {\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol}%
        \sbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox {\FV@SetupFont\Wrappedvisiblespace}%
        \def\FancyVerbFormatLine ##1{\hsize\linewidth
            \vtop{\raggedright\hyphenpenalty\z@\exhyphenpenalty\z@
                \doublehyphendemerits\z@\finalhyphendemerits\z@
                \strut ##1\strut}%
        }%
        % If the linebreak is at a space, the latter will be displayed as visible
        % space at end of first line, and a continuation symbol starts next line.
        % Stretch/shrink are however usually zero for typewriter font.
        \def\FV@Space {%
            \nobreak\hskip\z@ plus\fontdimen3\font minus\fontdimen4\font
            \discretionary{\copy\Wrappedvisiblespacebox}{\Wrappedafterbreak}
            {\kern\fontdimen2\font}%
        }%

        % Allow breaks at special characters using \PYG... macros.
        \Wrappedbreaksatspecials
        % Breaks at punctuation characters . , ; ? ! and / need catcode=\active
        \OriginalVerbatim[#1,codes*=\Wrappedbreaksatpunct]%
    }
    \makeatother

    % Exact colors from NB
    \definecolor{incolor}{HTML}{303F9F}
    \definecolor{outcolor}{HTML}{D84315}
    \definecolor{cellborder}{HTML}{CFCFCF}
    \definecolor{cellbackground}{HTML}{F7F7F7}

    % prompt
    \makeatletter
    \newcommand{\boxspacing}{\kern\kvtcb@left@rule\kern\kvtcb@boxsep}
    \makeatother
    \newcommand{\prompt}[4]{
        {\ttfamily\llap{{\color{#2}[#3]:\hspace{3pt}#4}}\vspace{-\baselineskip}}
    }
    

    
    % Prevent overflowing lines due to hard-to-break entities
    \sloppy
    % Setup hyperref package
    \hypersetup{
      breaklinks=true,  % so long urls are correctly broken across lines
      colorlinks=true,
      urlcolor=urlcolor,
      linkcolor=linkcolor,
      citecolor=citecolor,

    \textbf{init} initializing dataset objects, saves paths to images and
masks \textbf{len} PyTorch needs to know how many total items are in
your dataset so it knows when an epoch is finished

\textbf{getitem} can search for specific image, read it, use colour
palette, read masks, apply transformations

    The constructor of the standard
\texttt{ImageFolder\textquotesingle{}\ takes\ the}transform\texttt{parameter\ (and\ sometimes}target\_transform`).

They are used to convert uploaded images (usually \texttt{PIL.Image}) or
targets into tensors of the desired type. Torchvision includes the
transformations module for standard examples of such transformations.
Transformations can contain random transformations, which is the easiest
way to implement data augmentation. When defining a custom transformer,
in addition to the constructor, you only need to implement the
\texttt{\_\_call\_\_} method.:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\KeywordTok{class}\NormalTok{ HorizontalFlip(}\BuiltInTok{object}\NormalTok{):}
    \KeywordTok{def} \FunctionTok{\_\_init\_\_}\NormalTok{(}\VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{, mode}\OperatorTok{=}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{):}
        \VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{.method }\OperatorTok{=}\NormalTok{ mode}

    \KeywordTok{def} \FunctionTok{\_\_call\_\_}\NormalTok{(}\VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{, img):}
        \CommentTok{"""}
\CommentTok{        Args:}
\CommentTok{            img (PIL.Image): Image to be flipped.}

\CommentTok{        Returns:}
\CommentTok{            PIL.Image: Randomly flipped image.}
\CommentTok{        """}
        \ControlFlowTok{if} \VariableTok{self}\NormalTok{.method:}
            \ControlFlowTok{return}\NormalTok{ img.transpose(Image.FLIP\_LEFT\_RIGHT)}
        \ControlFlowTok{return}\NormalTok{ img}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]

    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.5}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{limit}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Configure random brightness jitter.}

\PY{k}{class}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nc}{ToTensorAndNormalizePair}\PY{p}{:}

    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}

\PY{l+s+sd}{            None}

        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{normalize} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{transforms}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Normalize}\PY{p}{(}
            \PY{n}{mean}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.485}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.456}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.406}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}

    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}call\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{image}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mask}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            image (PIL.Image.Image): RGB image.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            mask (PIL.Image.Image | None): Label mask, or None.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            tuple: ``(image\PYZus{}tensor, mask\PYZus{}tensor)`` with shapes ``[C,H,W]`` and ``[1,H,W]`` (mask).}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{n}{image} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to\PYZus{}tensor}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{image}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{image} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{normalize}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{image}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{mask\PYZus{}tensor} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{as\PYZus{}tensor}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mask}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dtype}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{float32}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mask\PYZus{}tensor}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{mask\PYZus{}tensor} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mask\PYZus{}tensor}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{unsqueeze}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{mask\PYZus{}tensor}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{max}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{mask\PYZus{}tensor} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mask\PYZus{}tensor} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mf}{255.0}

        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{image}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mask\PYZus{}tensor}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    This how we will add random transformations

            \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{\PYZus{}find\PYZus{}root}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{d}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{Path}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}

    When learning the network, it is more convenient to work with uploaders
rather than datasets. Loaders are created based on a dataset and allow
you to iterate over batches from it.

Pay attention to the \texttt{DataLoader} parameters. With
\texttt{num\_workers}\(\;> 1\), the batches are being prepared (images
are uploaded, processed, and so on) in several background processes at
once. Using the
\texttt{shuffle\textquotesingle{}\ parameter,\ you\ can\ submit\ images\ for\ training\ in\ random\ order.\ Usually,\ the\ data\ processing\ speed\ on\ the\ GPU\ exceeds\ the\ data\ loading\ speed\ in\ a\ single\ process,\ so\ the\ typical\ value\ for}num\_workers`
is\(\approx 3\text{-}10\).

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{9}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{build\PYZus{}preview\PYZus{}data\PYZus{}loaders}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}dataset}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}dataset}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{int} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{8}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}workers}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{int} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,}
\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{    }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Construct DataLoaders with fixed worker count (preview / exploration).}

\PY{l+s+sd}{    Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        train\PYZus{}dataset (Dataset): Training dataset.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        test\PYZus{}dataset (Dataset): Test dataset.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        batch\PYZus{}size (int): Batch size.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        num\PYZus{}workers (int): ``DataLoader`` workers.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{    Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        tuple[DataLoader, DataLoader]: ``(test\PYZus{}data\PYZus{}loader, train\PYZus{}data\PYZus{}loader)``.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{    \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}data\PYZus{}loader} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{DataLoader}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}dataset}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}workers}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}workers}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}data\PYZus{}loader} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{DataLoader}\PY{p}{(}
        \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}dataset}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}workers}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}workers}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{shuffle}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}
    \PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}data\PYZus{}loader}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}data\PYZus{}loader}


\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}data\PYZus{}loader}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}data\PYZus{}loader} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{build\PYZus{}preview\PYZus{}data\PYZus{}loaders}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}dataset}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}dataset}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    The loss function is implemented like all standard neural modules in
pytorch, via the
\texttt{torch.nn.Module\textquotesingle{}.\ In\ the\ cell\ below,\ you\ are\ asked\ to\ implement\ the\ loss\ function}dice`
(an analog of the Jacquard measure).

The result of \textbf{Dice Loss} is defined as:

\[
\text{Dice Coefficient} = 2\frac{|A \cap B| }{|A| + |B|} \leadsto \text{Dice Loss} = 1 - \frac{2\sum\limits_{i, j}a_{ij}b_{ij}}{\sum\limits_{ij}(a_{ij} + b_{ij} + \varepsilon)}
\]

where \(a_{ij} \in [0, 1]\) is the predicted probability of finding a
person in an image pixel, and \(b_{ij}\) is the true markup for an image
pixel.

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{10}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k}{class}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nc}{DiceLoss}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Module}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{eps}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{1e\PYZhy{}7}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{reduction}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{with\PYZus{}logits}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Dice loss for binary segmentation.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            eps (float): Small constant added to the denominator for stability.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            reduction (str | None): ``\PYZsq{}mean\PYZsq{}``, ``\PYZsq{}sum\PYZsq{}``, or ``None`` (per\PYZhy{}sample vector).}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            with\PYZus{}logits (bool): If True, apply sigmoid to ``logits`` before Dice.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            None}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{n+nb}{super}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{eps} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{eps}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reduction} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{reduction}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{with\PYZus{}logits} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{with\PYZus{}logits}

    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{forward}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{logits}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{true\PYZus{}labels}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Compute Dice loss between predictions and labels.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            logits (torch.Tensor): Shape ``[B, ...]``; logits or probabilities per ``with\PYZus{}logits``.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            true\PYZus{}labels (torch.Tensor): Binary (or integer) mask, same spatial shape as logits.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            torch.Tensor: Scalar if ``reduction`` is ``\PYZsq{}mean\PYZsq{}`` or ``\PYZsq{}sum\PYZsq{}``, else shape ``[B]``.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{n}{true\PYZus{}labels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{true\PYZus{}labels}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{long}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{with\PYZus{}logits}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{logits} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sigmoid}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{logits}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{logits\PYZus{}flat} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{logits}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{view}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{logits}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{true\PYZus{}labels\PYZus{}flat} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{true\PYZus{}labels}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{view}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{true\PYZus{}labels}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{intersection} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{logits\PYZus{}flat} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{true\PYZus{}labels\PYZus{}flat}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dim}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{denominator} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{logits\PYZus{}flat} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{true\PYZus{}labels\PYZus{}flat}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dim}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{eps}

        \PY{n}{loss\PYZus{}value} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{1.0} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mf}{2.0} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{intersection}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{denominator}

        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reduction} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sum}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{loss\PYZus{}value} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{loss\PYZus{}value}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reduction} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{mean}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{loss\PYZus{}value} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{loss\PYZus{}value}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reduction} \PY{o+ow}{is} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{k}{pass}

        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{loss\PYZus{}value}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    U-net schema

    

    Blocks of VGG13 looks like:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{    (}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{): Conv2d(...)}
\NormalTok{    (}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{): ReLU(...)}
\NormalTok{    (}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{): Conv2d(...)}
\NormalTok{    (}\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{): ReLU(...)}
\NormalTok{    (}\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{): MaxPool2d(...)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{activations}

    \paragraph{\texorpdfstring{\texttt{Decoder}}{Decoder}}\label{decoder}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{14}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k}{class}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nc}{DecoderBlock}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Module}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}One U\PYZhy{}Net decoder step: upsample, concat skip, two convs.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            out\PYZus{}channels (int): Channel width after this block.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            None}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{n+nb}{super}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{upconv} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Conv2d}\PY{p}{(}
            \PY{n}{in\PYZus{}channels}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{n}{kernel\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{padding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dilation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
        \PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{conv1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Conv2d}\PY{p}{(}
            \PY{n}{in\PYZus{}channels}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{n}{kernel\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{padding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dilation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
        \PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{conv2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Conv2d}\PY{p}{(}
            \PY{n}{in\PYZus{}channels}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{n}{kernel\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{padding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dilation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
        \PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{relu} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{ReLU}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{forward}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{down}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{left}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Fuse upsampled ``down`` with encoder skip ``left``.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            down (torch.Tensor): Deepest feature map being upsampled.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            left (torch.Tensor): Skip connection from encoder (same spatial size as upsampled ``down``).}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            torch.Tensor: Decoded features at this resolution.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{interpolate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{down}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{scale\PYZus{}factor}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mode}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{nearest}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{upconv}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cat}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{left}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dim}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{conv1}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{relu}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{conv2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{relu}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{x}
\end{Verbatim}

            \PY{n}{left} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{activations}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}
            \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{block}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{down}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{left}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{left}\PY{p}{)}

UNet(
  (encoder): VGG13Encoder(
    (blocks): ModuleList(
      (0): Sequential(
        (0): Conv2d(3, 64, kernel\_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1))
        (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
        (2): Conv2d(64, 64, kernel\_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1))
        (3): ReLU(inplace=True)
      )
      (1): Sequential(
        (0): Conv2d(64, 128, kernel\_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1))
        (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
        (2): Conv2d(128, 128, kernel\_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1))
        (3): ReLU(inplace=True)
      )
      (2): Sequential(
        (0): Conv2d(128, 256, kernel\_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1))
        (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
        (2): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel\_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1))
        (3): ReLU(inplace=True)
      )
    )
  )
  (decoder): ModuleList(
    (0): DecoderBlock(
      (upconv): Conv2d(256, 128, kernel\_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1,
1))
      (conv1): Conv2d(256, 128, kernel\_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1,
1))
      (conv2): Conv2d(128, 128, kernel\_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1,
1))
      (relu): ReLU()
    )
    (1): DecoderBlock(
      (upconv): Conv2d(128, 64, kernel\_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1,
1))
      (conv1): Conv2d(128, 64, kernel\_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1,
1))
      (conv2): Conv2d(64, 64, kernel\_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1))
      (relu): ReLU()
    )
  )
  (final): Conv2d(64, 1, kernel\_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))
)
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}
        
    Usually, the optimized functionality is difficult to interpret, and
different loss functions can be used in different experiments.
Therefore, it is necessary to measure and monitor an independent quality
metric. It is suggested to use \textbf{IoU (Intersection over Union)}
--- one of the standard options for the segmentation task: \[
\text{IoU} = \frac{|A \cap B|}{|A \cup B|} = \frac{\sum\limits_{ij}a_{ij}b_{ij}}{\sum\limits_{ij}a_{ij} + b_{ij} - a_{ij}b_{ij}}
\]

Note that the denominator can be zero, for example, if the mask is zero.
So projects can be implemented rather than studied, as otherwise metrics
are calculated at all levels. There are built-in devices for charging
using a mixer.

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{18}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k}{class}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nc}{IoUScore}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Module}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{threshold}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{reduction}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Per\PYZhy{}image IoU after thresholding (expects probabilities, not logits).}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            threshold (float): Binarization threshold on input values.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            reduction (str | None): ``\PYZsq{}mean\PYZsq{}``, ``\PYZsq{}sum\PYZsq{}``, or ``None`` (per\PYZhy{}batch vector).}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            None}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{n+nb}{super}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{threshold} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{threshold}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reduction} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{reduction}

    \PY{n+nd}{@torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{no\PYZus{}grad}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{forward}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{logits}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{true\PYZus{}labels}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Compute IoU between thresholded predictions and binarized targets.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            logits (torch.Tensor): Probabilities (e.g. after sigmoid), shape ``[B, ...]``.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            true\PYZus{}labels (torch.Tensor): Ground\PYZhy{}truth mask; values ``\PYZgt{} 0.5`` treated as foreground.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            torch.Tensor: Scalar if ``reduction`` is set, else shape ``[B]``.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{n}{preds} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{logits} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{threshold}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{view}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{logits}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{true\PYZus{}labels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{true\PYZus{}labels} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.5}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{view}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{true\PYZus{}labels}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{intersection} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{preds} \PY{o}{\PYZam{}} \PY{n}{true\PYZus{}labels}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dim}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{union} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{preds} \PY{o}{|} \PY{n}{true\PYZus{}labels}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dim}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{eps} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{1e\PYZhy{}7}
        \PY{n}{score} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{intersection} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{eps}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{union} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{eps}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reduction} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sum}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{score} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{score}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reduction} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{mean}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{score} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{score}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{score}

    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{pixel\PYZus{}accuracy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{probs}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{masks}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Mean per\PYZhy{}pixel agreement after thresholding.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            probs (torch.Tensor): Predicted probabilities in ``[0, 1]``.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            masks (torch.Tensor): Target mask (float), foreground if ``\PYZgt{} 0.5``.}

        \PY{n}{preds} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{probs} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.5}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{t} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{masks} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.5}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{preds} \PY{o}{==} \PY{n}{t}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{item}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{epoch} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{epochs}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{train}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}loss}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}iou}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}acc} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}

            \PY{n}{images}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{masks} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{images}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{masks}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{history}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{train\PYZus{}loss}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}loss} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}loader}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    \subsection{Save model}\label{save-model}

Persist Khoroshilova model weights and training histories under
\texttt{checkpoints/}.

    \textbf{IoU (Intersection over Union)} compares the predicted binary
mask \(A\) and the ground-truth mask \(B\):
\(\mathrm{IoU} = |A \cap B| / |A \cup B|\). It measures overlap (1 =
perfect). \textbf{Pixel accuracy} is the fraction of pixels where the
predicted class matches the label (0.5 threshold on probabilities). With
lots of background, pixel accuracy can look high even when the
foreground is wrong, so IoU is often the more informative metric for
segmentation.

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]

    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{forward}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{down}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{left}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Upsample ``down``, add skip ``left``, then convolve.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            down (torch.Tensor): Deep features to upsample.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            left (torch.Tensor): Encoder skip (same spatial size as upsampled ``down``).}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            torch.Tensor: Features for this decoder level.}

        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{interpolate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{down}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{scale\PYZus{}factor}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mode}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{nearest}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{upconv}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{relu}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{left}

        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{conv1}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{relu}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{conv2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{relu}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{x}

    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}classes}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}blocks}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}

        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{decoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{ModuleList}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}blocks} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}

        \PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{forward}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Encode with VGG13, decode with additive skips, then 1x1 head.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            x (torch.Tensor): Input ``[N, 3, H, W]``.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            torch.Tensor: Logits ``[N, num\PYZus{}classes, H, W]``.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{n}{activations} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{encoder}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{activations}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}

        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{block} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{enumerate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{decoder}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{left} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{activations}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}

        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{final}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{postprocess\PYZus{}mask}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mask\PYZus{}np}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}

\PY{l+s+sd}{    Args:}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        numpy.ndarray: Float32 binary mask ``\PYZob{}0, 1\PYZcb{}`` of the largest region, or ``mask\PYZus{}np`` if empty.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{    \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
    \PY{n}{labels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{measure}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{label}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mask\PYZus{}np} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.5}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{labels}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{max}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{mask\PYZus{}np}
    \PY{n}{region\PYZus{}sizes} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{bincount}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{labels}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{flat}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{largest\PYZus{}region\PYZus{}id} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{argmax}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{region\PYZus{}sizes}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
    \PY{n}{cleaned\PYZus{}mask} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{labels} \PY{o}{==} \PY{n}{largest\PYZus{}region\PYZus{}id}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{astype}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{float32}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{cleaned\PYZus{}mask}


\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{plot\PYZus{}linknet\PYZus{}postprocessed\PYZus{}grid}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{data\PYZus{}loader}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}images}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{int} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{    }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Compare raw sigmoid predictions vs largest\PYZhy{}component post\PYZhy{}processing.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{    Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        model (torch.nn.Module): Trained ``LinkNet``.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        data\PYZus{}loader (DataLoader): Test batches.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        device (torch.device): Inference device.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        num\PYZus{}images (int): Rows to display.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{    Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        None}
\PY{l+s+sd}{    \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
    \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{eval}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{images}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{true\PYZus{}masks} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{next}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{iter}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data\PYZus{}loader}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{images} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{images}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{with} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{no\PYZus{}grad}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{logits} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{images}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{preds} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sigmoid}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{logits}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{images\PYZus{}np} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{images}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cpu}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{permute}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{numpy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{preds\PYZus{}np} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{preds}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cpu}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{squeeze}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{numpy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mean} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.485}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.456}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.406}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{std} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.229}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.224}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.225}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{fig}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{axes} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{subplots}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}images}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{figsize}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{5} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}images}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}images}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{img} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{clip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{images\PYZus{}np}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{std} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{raw\PYZus{}prediction} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{preds\PYZus{}np}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{cleaned\PYZus{}prediction} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{postprocess\PYZus{}mask}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{raw\PYZus{}prediction}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{axes}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{imshow}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{img}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{axes}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{set\PYZus{}title}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Original Image}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{fontsize}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{14}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{axes}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{axis}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{off}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{axes}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{imshow}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{raw\PYZus{}prediction}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{cmap}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{gray}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{axes}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{set\PYZus{}title}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Raw Prediction (Before)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{fontsize}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{14}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{axes}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{imshow}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cleaned\PYZus{}prediction}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{cmap}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{gray}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{axes}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{set\PYZus{}title}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Cleaned Prediction (After)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{fontsize}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{14}\PY{p}{)}

    { \hspace*{\fill} \\}
    
    \section{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Safwan
Hossain}}{Safwan Hossain}}\label{safwan-hossain}

    \subsection{Encoder Fine-Tuning Strategy
Study}\label{encoder-fine-tuning-strategy-study}

The previous section trained both \textbf{U-Net} and \textbf{LinkNet}
end-to-end, meaning every layer (including the pretrained VGG13 encoder)
was updated by the optimizer from the first step.

This section investigates \textbf{how many encoder blocks should be
frozen} during training. Freezing early layers preserves low-level
ImageNet features (edges, textures) and reduces the number of trainable
parameters, while unfreezing deeper layers lets the model adapt
high-level representations to the segmentation task.

We also swap in a \textbf{regularized decoder} (BatchNorm + Dropout) to
see whether it improves generalization alongside the freeze strategy.

{\def\LTcaptype{table} % do not increment counter
\begin{longtable}[]{@{}lll@{}}
\toprule\noalign{}
Experiment & Frozen blocks & Decoder \\
\midrule\noalign{}
\endhead
\bottomrule\noalign{}
\endlastfoot
Full fine-tune & 0 & Regularized \\
Freeze 1 block & 1 & Regularized \\
Freeze 2 blocks & 2 & Regularized \\
Freeze 3 blocks & 3 & Regularized \\
\end{longtable}
}

    \subsubsection{Utility: freezing encoder
blocks}\label{utility-freezing-encoder-blocks}

\texttt{freeze\_encoder\_blocks(model,\ num\_blocks\_to\_freeze)}
disables gradient computation for the first \emph{N} encoder blocks,
keeping their pretrained ImageNet weights fixed during training.

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{31}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{freeze\PYZus{}encoder\PYZus{}blocks}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}blocks\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}freeze}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{    }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Freeze the first ``num\PYZus{}blocks\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}freeze`` VGG13 encoder blocks (``requires\PYZus{}grad=False``).}

\PY{l+s+sd}{    Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        model (torch.nn.Module): Model with ``model.encoder.blocks`` (e.g. ``UNet``, ``LinkNet``).}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        num\PYZus{}blocks\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}freeze (int): Number of initial encoder blocks to freeze; ``0`` freezes none.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{    Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        None: Prints trainable vs total parameter counts as a side effect.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{    \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{idx}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{block} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{enumerate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{encoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{blocks}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{requires\PYZus{}grad} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{idx} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}blocks\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}freeze}
        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{param} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{block}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{parameters}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{param}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{requires\PYZus{}grad} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{requires\PYZus{}grad}

    \PY{n}{frozen} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{b} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{encoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{blocks}
                 \PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n+nb}{next}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{b}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{parameters}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{requires\PYZus{}grad}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{trainable} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{p}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{numel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{p} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{parameters}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{p}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{requires\PYZus{}grad}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{total} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{p}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{numel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{p} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{parameters}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}
        \PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Encoder blocks frozen: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{frozen}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{/}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{encoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{blocks}\PY{p}{)}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ | }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Trainable params: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{trainable}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{,}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ / }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{total}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{,}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
    \PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \subsubsection{Regularized decoder: BatchNorm +
Dropout}\label{regularized-decoder-batchnorm-dropout}

We add \textbf{Batch Normalization} after each convolution (stabilizes
training, especially when parts of the encoder are frozen) and
\textbf{Dropout} (reduces overfitting when few parameters are being
trained).

The encoder stays the same pretrained \texttt{VGG13Encoder}; only the
decoder blocks change.

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{33}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k}{class}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nc}{RegularizedDecoderBlock}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Module}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{    }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Decoder block with BatchNorm after each conv and optional Dropout.\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}

    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dropout\PYZus{}p}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Build conv\PYZhy{}BN\PYZhy{}ReLU stack with optional spatial dropout.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            out\PYZus{}channels (int): Channel width for convolutions in this block.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            dropout\PYZus{}p (float): Dropout probability for ``Dropout2d``.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            None}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{n+nb}{super}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{upconv} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Conv2d}\PY{p}{(}
            \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{kernel\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{padding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{bn0} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{BatchNorm2d}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{conv1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Conv2d}\PY{p}{(}
            \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{kernel\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{padding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{bn1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{BatchNorm2d}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{conv2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Conv2d}\PY{p}{(}
            \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{kernel\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{padding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{bn2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{BatchNorm2d}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{relu} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{ReLU}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dropout} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Dropout2d}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{p}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{dropout\PYZus{}p}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{forward}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{down}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{left}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}U\PYZhy{}Net\PYZhy{}style upsample + concat skip with BN and dropout.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            down (torch.Tensor): Deep features to upsample.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            left (torch.Tensor): Encoder skip tensor.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            torch.Tensor: Decoded features at this resolution.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{F}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{interpolate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{down}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{scale\PYZus{}factor}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mode}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{nearest}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{relu}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{bn0}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{upconv}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cat}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{left}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dim}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{relu}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{bn1}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{conv1}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dropout}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{relu}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{bn2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{conv2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{x}


\PY{k}{class}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nc}{UNetRegularized}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Module}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{    }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}U\PYZhy{}Net with the same VGG13 encoder but a regularized decoder.\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}

    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}classes}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}blocks}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dropout\PYZus{}p}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Same encoder as ``UNet`` with batch\PYZhy{}norm and dropout in the decoder.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            num\PYZus{}classes (int): Channels for the final 1x1 conv.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            num\PYZus{}blocks (int): Encoder depth (VGG stages).}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            dropout\PYZus{}p (float): Dropout rate in each ``RegularizedDecoderBlock``.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            None}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{n+nb}{super}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{channels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{64}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{512}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{512}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{VGG13Encoder}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}blocks}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}blocks}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{decoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{ModuleList}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}blocks} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{decoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}
                \PY{n}{RegularizedDecoderBlock}\PY{p}{(}
                    \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}channels}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{channels}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dropout\PYZus{}p}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{dropout\PYZus{}p}\PY{p}{,}
                \PY{p}{)}
            \PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{final} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Conv2d}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{channels}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}classes}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{kernel\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{forward}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Run encoder, regularized decoder, and classification head.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            x (torch.Tensor): Input ``[N, 3, H, W]``.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{        Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{            torch.Tensor: Logits ``[N, num\PYZus{}classes, H, W]``.}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{n}{activations} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{encoder}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{activations}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{block} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{enumerate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{decoder}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{left} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{activations}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}
            \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{block}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{down}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{left}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{left}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{final}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}


\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{verify\PYZus{}unet\PYZus{}regularized\PYZus{}shape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{    }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Assert output shape and print parameter count for ``UNetRegularized``.}

\PY{l+s+sd}{    Args:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        None}

\PY{l+s+sd}{    Returns:}
\PY{l+s+sd}{        None}
\PY{l+s+sd}{    \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
    \PY{n}{\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{UNetRegularized}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}classes}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}blocks}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{\PYZus{}x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{randn}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{320}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{240}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{assert} \PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{\PYZus{}x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{320}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{240}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{UNetRegularized params: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n+nb}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{p}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{numel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{for}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n}{p}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{o+ow}{in}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n}{\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{parameters}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{,}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{del} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}x}

    \subsubsection{Fine-tuning experiments}\label{fine-tuning-experiments}

We train \texttt{UNetRegularized} under \textbf{4 freeze strategies},
all using the best loss from Khoroshilova's sweep (\textbf{BCE 0.2 +
Dice 0.8}) and \texttt{Adam(lr=1e-3)} for 5 epochs.

{\def\LTcaptype{table} % do not increment counter
\begin{longtable}[]{@{}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\linewidth - 2\tabcolsep) * \real{0.3182}}
  >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}p{(\linewidth - 2\tabcolsep) * \real{0.6818}}@{}}
\toprule\noalign{}
\begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Label
\end{minipage} & \begin{minipage}[b]{\linewidth}\raggedright
Blocks frozen
\end{minipage} \\
\midrule\noalign{}
\endhead
\bottomrule\noalign{}
\endlastfoot
Full fine-tune & 0 (baseline --- all encoder layers trainable) \\
Freeze 1 block & 1 (first 64-channel block frozen) \\
Freeze 2 blocks & 2 (64 + 128 blocks frozen) \\
Freeze all encoder & all encoder blocks frozen, only decoder + head
train \\
\end{longtable}
}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]

            \PY{n}{freeze\PYZus{}memory}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{strategy\PYZus{}name}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{peak\PYZus{}mb}
            \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Peak GPU memory: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{peak\PYZus{}mb}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.1f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ MB}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{Best strategy: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{freeze\PYZus{}best\PYZus{}strategy}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ with Test IoU = }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{freeze\PYZus{}best\PYZus{}iou}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{run\PYZus{}freeze\PYZus{}strategy\PYZus{}experiments}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}blocks}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{NUM\PYZus{}BLOCKS}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{epochs}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{show}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{model}


\PY{n}{best\PYZus{}freeze\PYZus{}model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{visualize\PYZus{}best\PYZus{}regularized\PYZus{}predictions}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{freeze\PYZus{}best\PYZus{}weights}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{freeze\PYZus{}best\PYZus{}strategy}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{freeze\PYZus{}best\PYZus{}iou}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{NUM\PYZus{}BLOCKS}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}loader}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{,}

\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{center}
    \adjustimage{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}{Human_Segmentation_files/Human_Segmentation_59_0.pdf}
    \end{center}
    { \hspace*{\fill} \\}
    
    \subsubsection{Interpretation \& Lessons I
Learned}\label{interpretation-lessons-i-learned}

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\item
  \textbf{Transfer learning depth matters.} The number of frozen encoder
  blocks directly affects convergence speed and final IoU. Freezing
  low-level feature blocks (edges, textures) usually preserves useful
  ImageNet representations without hurting segmentation quality.
\item
  \textbf{Regularized decoder.} Adding BatchNorm and Dropout to the
  decoder blocks (which Khoroshilova's original U-Net did not have)
  helps stabilize training, especially important when only a fraction of
  parameters are being updated (frozen-encoder scenarios).
\item
  \textbf{Practical GPU benefits.} Freezing encoder blocks reduces the
  number of gradient tensors stored during backpropagation, lowering
  peak GPU memory. This is valuable when training on consumer GPUs with
  limited VRAM.
\end{enumerate}

\textbf{Next steps:} - \textbf{Gradual unfreezing}: train decoder-only
for a few epochs, then progressively unfreeze encoder blocks with a
lower learning rate. - \textbf{Learning rate scheduling}: combine freeze
strategies with cosine annealing or step decay. - \textbf{More epochs}:
5 epochs may not fully reveal the gap between strategies; 15-20 epochs
would give clearer separation.

    Demo can be found in demo.ipynb
